namespace = HFP

## Expanded pregnancy events

########################################## MISSING REGENT WARNING ##################

# Pregnant ruler notified she hasn't appointed a regent
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20400
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20400
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery

	is_triggered_only = yes # various events in base_birth_events.txt

	ai = no

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20400 # I know just the guy

		trigger = {
			NOR = { # Not if you already have a regent
				has_assigned_minor_title = title_appointed_regent
				has_assigned_minor_title = title_regent
			}

			# Option only available if you have at least SOMEBODY that doesn't hate you in your court
			any_courtier_or_vassal = {
				is_adult = yes
				prisoner = no
				is_incapable = no
				has_regent = no

				OR = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value >= 20
					}

					is_friend = ROOT
					is_lover = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				prisoner = no
				is_incapable = no
				has_regent = no

				OR = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value >= 20
					}

					is_friend = ROOT
					is_lover = ROOT
				}
			}

			# First search for person who both likes you, is trustworthy, and is competent
			preferred_limit = {
				stewardship >= 10

				OR = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value >= 50
					}

					is_friend = ROOT
					is_lover = ROOT
				}

				NOR = {
					trait = deceitful
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}

			# Then search for person who likes you and is trustworthy
			preferred_limit = {
				OR = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value >= 30
					}

					is_friend = ROOT
					is_lover = ROOT
				}

				NOR = {
					trait = deceitful
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}

			# Then search for person that likes you

			give_minor_title = title_appointed_regent
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20400 # I'll think about it
	}

	after = {
		set_dynasty_flag = pregnancy_regent_warning
	}
}

# on_pregnancy, set clock for finishing phase at 2 months
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20401

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_pregnancy
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		character_event = {
			id = HFP.20402
			days = 170
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = HFP.20402

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = pregnant

		has_game_rule = {
			name = pregnancy_flavor
			value = on
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		add_trait = pregnancy_finishing
	}
}

# on_birth (fired on the child), remove the trait and check all flavor flags
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20403

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_birth
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		mother = {
			remove_trait = pregnancy_finishing
			remove_trait = in_hiding
			remove_trait = travelling
			remove_character_modifier = mother_praying_health
			remove_character_modifier = mother_resting_health
			remove_character_modifier = mother_partying_health
			clr_character_flag = mother_asked_retirement
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_dark_rest

			# Safety check, they should already have been removed
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_listening
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_talking
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_trusting
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_plotting
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_envious
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_shy
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_learning
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_content
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_gluttonous

			character_event = {
				id = HFP.20597 # Clears persistent Physician targets. They are still on on_birth since post-partum complications may require their services
				days = 35
			}
		}

		# Mother took part in fertility feast, chance of blessed girl
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				NOT = { trait = attractive }

				mother = {
					has_character_modifier = mother_fertility_festival_2
				}
			}

			random_list = {
				40 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = ugly }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = ugly }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = attractive }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = attractive }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						mother_even_if_dead = { any_child = { trait = attractive } } # Avoid entire litters of them
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						father_even_if_dead = { any_child = { trait = attractive } } # Avoid entire litters of them
					}
				}

				60 = {
					remove_trait = hunchback
					remove_trait = dwarf
					remove_trait = ugly
					remove_trait = inbred
					remove_trait = sickly
					remove_trait = harelip
					remove_trait = lisp

					mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20055 days = 3600 random = 200 } }
					father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20055 days = 3600 random = 200 } }
				}
			}
		}

		# Catholic/Orthodox Kings/Emperors: chance for special baptism
		father = { save_event_target_as = scoped_father }
		mother = { save_event_target_as = scoped_mother }

		event_target:scoped_father = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = event_target:scoped_mother }
						is_married_matrilineally = no
					}
					trigger_else = {
						higher_tier_than = event_target:scoped_mother
					}
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = HF.20100
				days = 12
			}
		}

		event_target:scoped_mother = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = event_target:scoped_father }
						is_married_matrilineally = yes
					}
					trigger_else = {
						higher_tier_than = event_target:scoped_father
					}
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = HF.20100
				days = 12
			}
		}

		clear_event_target = scoped_father
		clear_event_target = scoped_mother

		# Catholic/Orthodox rulers: chance of Churching after the first pregnancy is over
		mother = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = catholic
						religion = orthodox
					}

					is_married = yes
					num_of_children < 2

					OR = {
						is_ruler = yes
						spouse = { is_ruler = yes }
					}

					NOR = {
						society_member_of = the_satanists
						has_character_modifier = adulteress
						has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
					}
				}

				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20018
					days = 24
				}
			}
		}

		# Mother drunk/had drugs during pregnancy, chance of dumb child
		if = {
			limit = {
				mother = {
					trait = drunkard
				}
			}

			random = {
				chance = 30

				set_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth

				if = {
					limit = { trait = slow }

					remove_trait = slow
					add_trait = imbecile
					mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20001 days = 451 } }
					father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20002 days = 450 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { trait = quick }
					remove_trait = quick
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { trait = genius }
					remove_trait = genius
					add_trait = quick
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { trait = imbecile } }

					add_trait = slow
					mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20001 days = 451 } }
					father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20002 days = 450 } }
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				mother = {
					has_character_modifier = hashish_addict
				}
			}

			random = {
				chance = 30

				set_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth

				if = {
					limit = { trait = slow }

					remove_trait = slow
					add_trait = imbecile
					mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20001 days = 451 } }
					father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20002 days = 450 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { trait = quick }
					remove_trait = quick
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { trait = genius }
					remove_trait = genius
					add_trait = quick
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { trait = imbecile } }

					add_trait = slow
					mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20001 days = 451 } }
					father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20002 days = 450 } }
				}
			}
		}

		random_list = { # Chance of imprinting (mother)
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					mother = { num_of_children >= 2 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.35
					mother = { num_of_children >= 3 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					mother = { num_of_children >= 4 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					mother = { num_of_children >= 5 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					mother = { practical_age >= 30 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					mother = { trait = kind }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					mother = { trait = charitable }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					mother = { trait = envious }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					mother = { trait = cruel }
				}

				mother = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20599
						days = 70
					}
				}
			}

			50 = { }
		}

		random_list = { # Chance of imprinting (father)
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					father = { num_of_children >= 2 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.35
					father = { num_of_children >= 3 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					father = { num_of_children >= 4 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					father = { num_of_children >= 5 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					father = { practical_age >= 30 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					father = { trait = kind }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					father = { trait = charitable }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					father = { trait = envious }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					father = { trait = cruel }
				}

				father = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20000
						days = 700
						random = 500
					}
				}
			}

			50 = { }
		}

		mother = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = flag_vatican_prince } # The Papal orgy bears fruits

				clr_character_flag = flag_vatican_prince

				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20598 # Notify mother
					days = 7
					random = 7
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }

				random = {
					chance = 80
					ROOT = { set_character_flag = flag_troubled_pregnancy_child }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { trait = stressed }

				random = {
					chance = 30

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20581 # Chance to recover from stressed
						days = 30
						random = 50
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = mother_craved_quail }

				clr_character_flag = mother_craved_quail

				random = {
					chance = 70

					ROOT = { add_trait = clubfooted }

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20582 # Notify mother child gains 2 diplomacy
						days = 950
						random = 550
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = mother_craved_hare }

				clr_character_flag = mother_craved_hare

				random = {
					chance = 70

					ROOT = { add_trait = harelip }

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20583 # Notify mother child gains 2 intrigue
						days = 950
						random = 550
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = mother_craved_trout }

				clr_character_flag = mother_craved_trout

				random = {
					chance = 70

					ROOT = { add_trait = ugly }

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20584 # Notify mother child gains 2 learning
						days = 950
						random = 550
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				mother = { has_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_warrior }
			}

			mother = { clr_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_warrior }

			# Small chance of child actually gaining positive trait
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = weak }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = frail }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = inbred }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = hunchback }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = dwarf }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = weak }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = frail }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = inbred }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = hunchback }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = dwarf }
					}

					if = {
						limit = { trait = weak }
						remove_trait = weak
					}
					if = {
						limit = { trait = frail }
						remove_trait = frail
					}
					if = {
						limit = { trait = inbred }
						remove_trait = inbred
					}
					if = {
						limit = { trait = hunchback }
						remove_trait = hunchback
					}
					if = {
						limit = { trait = dwarf }
						remove_trait = dwarf
					}
					if = {
						limit = { trait = sickly }
						remove_trait = sickly
					}

					mother = {
						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20585 # Notify mother child gains 2 martial
							days = 250
							random = 250
						}
					}
				}

				80 = { } # No luck
			}
		}

		# Mother offered sacrifice for strong child
		if = {
			limit = {
				mother = { has_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_strong }
			}

			mother = { clr_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_strong }

			# Small chance of child actually gaining positive trait
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = weak }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = frail }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = inbred }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = hunchback }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = dwarf }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = weak }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = frail }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = inbred }
					}

					remove_trait = weak
					remove_trait = sickly
					add_trait = strong

					mother = {
						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20586 # Notify mother child is growing strong
							days = 250
							random = 250
						}
					}
				}

				80 = { # No luck
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = strong }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = strong }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		# Mother offered sacrifice for pretty child
		if = {
			limit = {
				mother = { has_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_pretty }
			}

			mother = { clr_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_pretty }

			# Small chance of child actually gaining positive trait
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = ugly }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = attractive }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = ugly }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = attractive }
					}

					remove_trait = harelip
					remove_trait = ugly
					add_trait = attractive

					mother = {
						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20587 # Notify mother child is growing strong
							days = 250
							random = 250
						}
					}
				}

				80 = { } # No luck
			}
		}

		# Mother offered sacrifice for smart child
		if = {
			limit = {
				mother = { has_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_smart }
			}

			mother = { clr_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_smart }

			# Small chance of child actually gaining positive trait
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = slow }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.25
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = imbecile }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = quick }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						mother_even_if_dead = { trait = genius }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = slow }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.25
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = imbecile }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = ugly }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = quick }
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						father_even_if_dead = { trait = genius }
					}

					remove_trait = slow
					remove_trait = imbecile

					if = {
						limit = { trait = quick }

						remove_trait = quick
						add_trait = genius
					}
					else = {
						add_trait = quick
					}

					mother = {
						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20588 # Notify mother child is growing smart
							days = 450
							random = 450
						}
					}
				}
				80 = { } # No luck
			}
		}

		# Mother wanted a boy/girl
		mother = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_boy
						has_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_girl
					}
				}

				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20589 # Did the bet pay out?
					days = 15
					random = 15
				}
			}
		}

		# Mother made a vow to the Holy Virgin
		if = {
			limit = {
				mother = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity
						has_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility
						has_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity
						has_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance
					}
				}
			}

			# Possible divine intervention
			random_list = {
				70 = { } # Nothing happens

				30 = {
					# Broke the vow, decreased chance
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance

							OR = {
								trait = gluttonous
								trait = hedonist
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity
							trait = greedy
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility
							trait = proud
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity
							trait = lustful
						}
					}


					# Remained true to the vow, increased chance

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance
							trait = temperate
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity
							trait = charitable
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility
							trait = humble
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75

						mother = {
							has_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity

							OR = {
								trait = chaste
								trait = celibate
							}
						}
					}

					remove_trait = sickly
					remove_trait = inbred
					remove_trait = harelip
					remove_trait = clubfooted
					remove_trait = hunchback
					remove_trait = lisp
					remove_trait = stutter
					remove_trait = ugly
					remove_trait = dwarf
					remove_trait = slow
					remove_trait = imbecile
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}

			mother = {
				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20590 # Did it work? If so, does she keep her word?
					days = 25
					random = 25
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hard pregnancy starts
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20404
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20404
	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news_female

	is_triggered_only = yes # various events in base_birth_events.txt

	trigger = {
		trait = pregnant
	}

	immediate = {
		add_trait = hard_pregnancy
	}

	option = { # Abort
		name = EVTOPTZHFP20404

		trigger = {
			is_playable = yes

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_married = yes }
				is_married_matrilineally = yes
			}

			NOR = {
				trait = kind

				AND = {
					religion_group = christian
					trait = zealous
				}
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = { text = tooltip_20404_abortion }

		tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes
		remove_trait = hard_pregnancy
		remove_trait = pregnant

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = aborted_child
			years = 4
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_pregnancy = yes

			random_list = {
				25 = { character_event = { id = HFP.20064 days = 35 } } # Mother becomes depressed/insane
				25 = { character_event = { id = HFP.20065 days = 35 } } # Mother accidentally reveals the deed
				25 = { character_event = { id = HFP.20066 days = 35 } } # Mother permanently loses fertility
				25 = { } # Nothing happens
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					is_married = yes
					NOT = { has_religion_feature = religion_matriarchal }

					spouse = {
						is_incapable = no
						is_inaccessible_trigger = no

						NOR = {
							trait = slow
							trait = imbecile
							trait = trusting
							trait = inbred
						}
					}
				}

				spouse = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20061
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			trigger = {
				NOT = { trait = brave }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = craven
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_religion_feature = religion_matriarchal
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cruel
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = envious
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20404

		tooltip = {
			add_trait = hard_pregnancy
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_married = yes }

				spouse = {
					character_event = { id = HFP.20405 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician }

				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = { has_minor_title = title_court_physician }
					character_event = { id = HFP.20405 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20407 # If lonely, decide if to temporarily retire from rule
					days = 6
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 99 }
	}
}

# Became wroth pregnant
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20413
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20413
	picture = GFX_evt_quarrel

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = hard_pregnancy
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20413

		if = {
			limit = { trait = wroth } # If you already have the bad trait before this event, small chance of troubled pregnancy

			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 1

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = stressed
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = frail
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = weak
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						is_ill = yes
					}

					troubled_pregnancy_chance_low_effect = yes # Critical Failure: chance of Troubled Pregnancy
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_character_flag = wroth_pregnant # Check to see if trait is temporary, so that after pregnancy is over there is greater chance of recovery
			add_trait = wroth
		}

		character_event = { id = HFP.20442 days = 5 random = 10 } # Confirmation
		character_event = { id = HFP.20422 days = 200 } # Post-pregnancy recovery
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20413

		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }

			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 20

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = stressed
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = frail
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = weak
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						is_ill = yes
					}

					troubled_pregnancy_chance_low_effect = yes # Critical Failure: chance of Troubled Pregnancy
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 40

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = stressed
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = paranoid
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = patient # Countertrait
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					trait = kind
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = wroth
				}

				tooltip = {
					add_trait = depressed
				}

				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20415 # Depressed pregnant
					days = 5
					random = 5
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Became gluttonous pregnant
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20414
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20414
	picture = GFX_evt_fancy_feast

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { trait = hard_pregnancy }

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20414

		if = {
			limit = { trait = gluttonous } # If you already have the bad trait before this event, small chance of troubled pregnancy

			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 1

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = stressed
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = frail
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = weak
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						is_ill = yes
					}

					troubled_pregnancy_chance_low_effect = yes  # Critical Failure: chance of Troubled Pregnancy.
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 40
				add_trait_fully_gluttonous_effect = yes
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = gluttonous_pregnant } }

			character_event = { id = HFP.20441 days = 15 random = 10 } # Confirmation
			character_event = { id = HFP.20421 days = 200 } # Post-pregnancy recovery
		}

		set_character_flag = gluttonous_pregnant # Avoid double event if fired by weird cravings, facilitate post-birth recovery
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20414

		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }

			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 20

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = stressed
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = frail
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = weak
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						is_ill = yes
					}

					troubled_pregnancy_chance_low_effect = yes # Critical Failure: chance of Troubled Pregnancy
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 40

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = stressed
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = paranoid
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = temperate # Countertrait
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					trait = hedonist
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gluttonous
				}

				tooltip = {
					add_trait = depressed
				}

				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20415 # Depressed pregnant
					days = 5
					random = 5
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

				trait = duelist
			}
		}

		add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes

	}

# Countryside: Health is dropping during travel
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20418
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20418
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { trait = hard_pregnancy }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_court_physician }
				save_event_target_as = localize_physician
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Knows how to treat herself
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20418
		tooltip_info = learning

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				learning >= 15
				trait = scholar
				trait = gardener
				trait = mystic
				trait = physician
			}
		}

		health = -0.25
		troubled_pregnancy_chance_low_effect = yes # Critical failure: chance of Troubled Pregnancy

		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
	}

	option = { # Ask my Physician
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20418

		trigger = { has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician }

		show_portrait = event_target:localize_physician
		wealth = -15
		health = -0.25

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = { # Ask my spouse's Physician
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20418

		trigger = {
			is_ruler = no

			spouse = {
				has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician
			}
		}

		health = -0.25

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDHFP20418

		trigger = {
			learning < 15

			NOR = {
				trait = scholar
				trait = gardener
				trait = mystic
				trait = physician
				has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician
				spouse = { has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician }
			}
		}

		health = -0.75
		troubled_pregnancy_chance_medium_effect = yes # Critical failure: chance of Troubled Pregnancy

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}
}

# HFP.20500 Troubled Pregnancy begins
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20500
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20500
	picture = GFX_evt_illness

	is_triggered_only = yes # troubled_pregnancy_chance_low/medium_effect

	immediate = {
		remove_trait = hard_pregnancy
		add_trait = troubled_pregnancy
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20500

		tooltip = {
			add_trait = troubled_pregnancy
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			# Used to determine if the mother dies or not, and if there are complications after the pregnancy
			set_variable = {
				which = troubled_pregnancy_variable
				value = 2
			}

			if = { # If married, spouse may offer assistance
				limit = { is_married = yes }

				spouse = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20501
						days = 4
					}
				}
			}

			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_regent
						has_minor_title = title_appointed_regent
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value < -50
						}
					}

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20502 # If regent doesn't like you, he may try to kill you in your vulnerable state
						days = 3
						random = 3
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_married = FROM } } # Don't fire twice if the spouse is also the regent

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20501 # If regent likes you, he'll try to help you, as if he were your spouse
						days = 6
					}
				}
			}

			if = { # Chance of a strange birth
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion_group = christian
						religion_group = muslim
						religion_openly_tengri_or_reformed_trigger = yes
						religion_openly_norse_or_reformed_trigger = yes
					}

					NOT = { has_dynasty_flag = flag_vision_baby }
				}

				random_list = {
					70 = { }

					15 = {
						set_dynasty_flag = flag_vision_baby # Positive
						character_event = { id = HFP.20503 days = 43 random = 20 }
					}

					15 = {
						set_dynasty_flag = flag_vision_baby # Negative
						character_event = { id = HFP.20504 days = 33 random = 20 }
					}
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = HFP.20520 # Give mom chance to help herself
				days = 10
				random = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

# Notify Spouse and Regent of the ruler about what is happening and prompt either to offer help if possible
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20501

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20501
		picture = GFX_evt_bad_news
		trigger = { is_married = FROM }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20501
		picture = GFX_evt_illness
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_minor_title = title_regent
				has_minor_title = title_appointed_regent
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Send Physician
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20501

		trigger = { has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician }

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = EVTOOLTIPAHFP20501

			if = {
				limit = { is_married = FROM }

				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = { has_minor_title = title_court_physician }
					save_event_target_as = pregnancy_spouse_physician
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = { has_minor_title = title_court_physician }
					save_event_target_as = pregnancy_regent_physician
				}
			}

			FROM = {
				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20505 # Notify woman
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}

		wealth = -50

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					trait = quick
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					trait = genius
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					learning >= 20
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					learning < 10
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Send Physician (no Reaper's Due)
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20501

		trigger = {
			is_ruler = yes
			FROM = { is_ruler = no }
			NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
		}

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = EVTOOLTIPAHFP20501
			FROM = { set_character_flag = pregnancy_healer_help }
		}

		wealth = -50

		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
	}

	option = { # No Physician, but I am a Scholar myself
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20501

		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOOLTIPBHFP20501 }

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = scholar
				trait = mystic
				trait = physician
				learning >= 15
			}

			NOT = { has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician }
			is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_married = FROM }
			save_event_target_as = pregnancy_spouse_physician
		}
		else = {
			save_event_target_as = pregnancy_regent_physician
		}

		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = HFP.20506 } # Notify woman
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = quick
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = genius
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				learning >= 20
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				learning < 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Send a Priest
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20501

		trigger = {
			is_not_unreformed_pagan_trigger = yes

			FROM = {
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
					has_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
				}
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOOLTIPCHFP20501 }

		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
				character_event = { id = HFP.20509 } # Notify woman
			}
		}

		piety = 100
		wealth = -20

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Send a Shaman
		name = EVTOPTDHFP20501
		trigger = {
			is_unreformed_pagan_trigger = yes

			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
					has_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
				}
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOOLTIPDHFP20501 }

		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
				character_event = { id = HFP.20510 } # Notify woman
			}
		}

		piety = 50
		prestige = 50
		wealth = -5

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_tribal = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				is_nomadic = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Offer moral support
		name = EVTOPTEHFP20501

		trigger = { is_married = FROM }

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = pregnancy_spouse_comfort

			character_event = {
				id = HFP.20519 # Notify woman
				tooltip = EVTOOLTIPEHFP20501
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value >= -50
					}
				}

				opinion = {
					name = comforted_opinion
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1

				# If you have a better option, you'd need to be an idiot not use that
				OR = {
					trait = zealous
					trait = cruel
					has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician

					AND = {
						is_inaccessible_trigger = no
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no

						OR = {
							trait = scholar
							trait = mystic
							trait = physician
							learning >= 15
						}
					}
				}

				NOR = {
					trait = slow
					trait = imbecile
					trait = inbred
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Do nothing
		name = EVTOPTFHFP20501

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_lover = FROM
					is_friend = FROM
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 50
				is_rival = FROM
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10

				trait = greedy
				wealth < 0
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10

				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 30

				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value < -90
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		text = EVTDESCHFPB20503
		picture = GFX_evt_comet
		trigger = { religion_openly_norse_or_reformed_trigger = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPC20503
		picture = GFX_evt_wolf
		trigger = { religion_openly_tengri_or_reformed_trigger = yes }

			}

# Spouse/Regent has sent his physician to help. Do you want him?
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20505
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20505
	picture = GFX_evt_court_physician

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = troubled_pregnancy
		trait = pregnant
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20505

		if = {
			limit = { event_target:pregnancy_spouse_physician = { always = yes } }

			save_persistent_event_target = {
				name = pregnancy_spouse_physician_per
				scope = event_target:pregnancy_spouse_physician
			}
		}
		else = {
			save_persistent_event_target = {
				name = pregnancy_regent_physician_per
				scope = event_target:pregnancy_regent_physician
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_relieved
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20507 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_married = FROM
				event_target:pregnancy_spouse_physician = { learning < 10 }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { is_married = FROM }
				event_target:pregnancy_regent_physician = { learning < 10 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20505

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_worried
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20508 }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_married = FROM }
				clear_event_target = pregnancy_spouse_physician
			}
			else = {

	picture = GFX_evt_library

		trait = troubled_pregnancy
		trait = pregnant
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20506

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_relieved
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20507 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { event_target:pregnancy_spouse_physician = { always = yes } }

			save_persistent_event_target = {
				name = pregnancy_spouse_physician_per
				scope = event_target:pregnancy_spouse_physician
			}
		}
		else = {
			save_persistent_event_target = {
				name = pregnancy_regent_physician_per
				scope = event_target:pregnancy_regent_physician
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { learning < 10 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20506

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_worried
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20508 }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_married = FROM }
				clear_event_target = pregnancy_spouse_physician
			}
			else = {
				clear_event_target = pregnancy_regent_physician
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			trigger = { is_ruler = yes }

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_rival = FROM
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = HFP.20520
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20520
	picture = GFX_evt_illness

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # My Physician will help me
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20520

		trigger = { has_assigned_minor_title = title_court_physician }

		wealth = -50

		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = { has_minor_title = title_court_physician }

			ROOT = {
				save_persistent_event_target = {
					name = pregnancy_mother_physician_per
					scope = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					trait = quick
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					trait = genius
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					learning >= 20
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					learning < 10
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Call for a Healer (don't have Physicians due to lack of Reaper's Due DLC)
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20520

		trigger = {
			is_ruler = yes
			NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
		}

		set_character_flag = pregnancy_healer_help
		wealth = -50

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Call for a Priest
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20520

		trigger = {
			is_ruler = yes
			is_not_unreformed_pagan_trigger = yes

			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort # Already taken from the spouse/regent
				has_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
		piety = 100
		wealth = -20

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Call for a Shaman
		name = EVTOPTDHFP20520

		trigger = {
			is_ruler = yes
			is_unreformed_pagan_trigger = yes

			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort # Already taken from the spouse/regent
				has_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
		piety = 50
		prestige = 50
		wealth = -5

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_tribal = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				is_nomadic = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Do nothing
		name = EVTOPTEHFP20520
	}

	after = { # Now for randomized pain
		character_event = {
			id = HFP.20521
			days = 15
			random = 15
		}
	}
}

					persistent_event_target:pregnancy_regent_physician_per = { learning >= 25 }
				}

				# Every successful healing on random event reduces variable, lower the variable, more likely mother is to recover.
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= -1 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= -2 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= -4 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= -6 }
				}

				character_event = { id = HFP.20536 } # RECOVERY
			}

			1 = {
				# Every failed healing on random event increases variable, higher the variable, more likely mother is to die
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= 1 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= 2 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= 3 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= 4 }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 3
					check_variable = { which = troubled_pregnancy_variable value >= 5 }
				}

				character_event = { id = HFP.20537 } # DEATH
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }

			if = {
				limit = { trait = cough }
				health = -0.05
			}

				add_trait = cough
			}
		}
		else = {

		}

# Troubled pregnancy: Recovery
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20536
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20536	# Possible custom loc keys added to describe help from spouse/physicians/priests
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = troubled_pregnancy
		trait = pregnant
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_trait = cough
		remove_trait = fever
		remove_trait = vomiting
		remove_trait = cramps
		remove_trait = rash
		remove_trait = headache
		remove_trait = fatigue
		remove_trait = malaise
		remove_trait = infection
		remove_trait = stressed
		health = 0.1
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20536

		hidden_effect = {
			# Not set to 0, still small chance of post-birth complications
			change_variable = {
				which = troubled_pregnancy_variable
				value = -4
			}

			clr_character_flag = pregnancy_healer_help
			clr_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
			clr_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
			clr_character_flag = pregnancy_spouse_comfort
			clr_character_flag = mother_asked_retirement

			# Send notifications to all doctors
			persistent_event_target:pregnancy_mother_physician_per = { character_event = { id = HFP.20553 } }
			persistent_event_target:pregnancy_spouse_physician_per = { character_event = { id = HFP.20553 } }
			persistent_event_target:pregnancy_regent_physician_per = { character_event = { id = HFP.20553 } }

			# And to the spouse, if he already isn't one of them
			if = {
				limit = {
					persistent_event_target:pregnancy_mother_physician_per = { NOT = { is_married = ROOT } }
					persistent_event_target:pregnancy_spouse_physician_per = { NOT = { is_married = ROOT } }
					persistent_event_target:pregnancy_regent_physician_per = { NOT = { is_married = ROOT } }
				}

				spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20554 } }
			}
		}

		remove_trait = troubled_pregnancy
		set_character_flag = survivor_mom # More likely to have difficult pregnancies in the future, unlocks chance to go celibate for rulers
	}
}

# Troubled pregnancy: DEATH before birth
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20537
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20537
	picture = GFX_evt_illness

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = troubled_pregnancy
		trait = pregnant
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20537

		hidden_effect = {
			remove_trait = cough
			remove_trait = fever
			remove_trait = diarrhea
			remove_trait = vomiting
			remove_trait = chest_pain
			remove_trait = cramps
			remove_trait = rash
			remove_trait = headache
			remove_trait = abdominal_pain
			remove_trait = fatigue
			remove_trait = malaise
			remove_trait = infection
		}

		spouse = { save_event_target_as = scoped_father }

		# Hollow child is born in this circumstance, giving another chance to avoid game over
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = tooltip_HFP20537_A

			create_character = {
				random_traits = no
				dynasty = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				female = 50
				age = 0
			}

			new_character = {
				set_mother = ROOT

				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = clubfooted
				}

				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = ugly
				}

				lose_weight_large_effect = yes
				lose_weight_medium_effect = yes
				add_trait = malnourished
				save_event_target_as = hollow_baby
				set_character_flag = flag_hollow_child_primed

				if = { # If a dad exists...
					limit = { event_target:scoped_father = { always = yes } }

					set_father = event_target:scoped_father

					if = { # and mom is not matrilineally married...
						limit = { ROOT = { is_married_matrilineally = no } }

						event_target:hollow_baby = {
							dynasty = event_target:scoped_father
							culture = event_target:scoped_father
							religion = event_target:scoped_father
						}
					}
				}
			}

			event_target:scoped_father = { # Check if father likes mother
				if = {
					limit = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value >= 40
						}
					}

					set_character_flag = flag_loved_dead_mother
				}

				character_event = { id = HFP.20056 }
			}

			death = { death_reason = death_troubled_pregnancy }
		}
	}
}

# on_birth baby vision child event
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20538
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20538
	picture = GFX_evt_comet

	is_triggered_only = yes # 313, base_birth_events.txt

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20538 # Yay! I'm vision baby!"

		if = {
			limit = { mother = { has_character_flag = gabriel_baby } }

			mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20539 days = 1 } }
			father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20539 days = 1 } }

			change_diplomacy = 2
			remove_trait = hunchback
			remove_trait = dwarf
			remove_trait = inbred
			remove_trait = lisp
			remove_trait = stutter
			remove_trait = freckles
			remove_trait = clubfooted
			remove_trait = slow
			remove_trait = imbecile
			remove_trait = harelip
			remove_trait = ugly
			remove_trait = weak
			remove_trait = sickly

			random_list = {
				50 = {
					trigger = {
						NOT = { trait = attractive }
					}

					add_trait = attractive
				}

				50 = {
					trigger = {
						NOR = {
							trait = genius
							trait = quick
						}
					}

					add_trait = quick
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { mother = { has_character_flag = lucifer_baby } }

			mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }
			father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }

			change_intrigue = 1
			add_trait = lefthanded
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { mother = { has_character_flag = iblis_baby } }

			mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }
			father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }

			change_learning = 1
			add_trait = hunchback
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { mother = { has_character_flag = thor_baby } }

			mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20539 days = 1 } }
			father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20539 days = 1 } }

			change_martial = 2
			remove_trait = hunchback
			remove_trait = dwarf
			remove_trait = inbred
			remove_trait = lisp
			remove_trait = stutter
			remove_trait = freckles
			remove_trait = clubfooted
			remove_trait = slow
			remove_trait = imbecile
			remove_trait = harelip
			remove_trait = ugly
			remove_trait = weak
			remove_trait = sickly
			add_trait = strong
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { mother = { has_character_flag = loki_baby } }

			mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }
			father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }

			change_intrigue = 1
			add_trait = blinded
			add_trait = giant
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { mother = { has_character_flag = tengri_baby } }

			mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20539 days = 1 } }
			father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20539 days = 1 } }

			change_martial = 2
			remove_trait = hunchback
			remove_trait = dwarf
			remove_trait = inbred
			remove_trait = lisp
			remove_trait = stutter
			# remove_trait = freckles
			remove_trait = clubfooted
			remove_trait = slow
			remove_trait = imbecile
			remove_trait = harelip
			remove_trait = ugly
			remove_trait = weak
			remove_trait = sickly
			add_trait = shrewd
		}
		if = {
			limit = { mother = { has_character_flag = erlik_baby } }

			mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }
			father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20540 days = 1 } }

			change_stewardship = 1
			add_trait = frail
		}
	}
}

# Complete recovery
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20544
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20544
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = troubled_pregnancy
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_trait = cough
		remove_trait = fever
		remove_trait = vomiting
		remove_trait = cramps
		remove_trait = rash
		remove_trait = headache
		remove_trait = fatigue
		remove_trait = malaise
		remove_trait = infection
		remove_trait = stressed
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_healer_help
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_spouse_comfort
		clr_character_flag = mother_asked_retirement
		set_character_flag = survivor_mom
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20544 # I won't mind getting up now

		remove_trait = troubled_pregnancy

		spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20548 } }
	}
}

# Partial recovery
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20545
	desc = EVTDESCHFP20545
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = troubled_pregnancy
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_trait = cough
		remove_trait = fever
		remove_trait = vomiting
		remove_trait = cramps
		remove_trait = rash
		remove_trait = headache
		remove_trait = fatigue
		remove_trait = malaise
		remove_trait = infection
		remove_trait = stressed
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_healer_help
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_spouse_comfort
		clr_character_flag = mother_asked_retirement
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20545 # I think I'll rest another couple of days still...

		if = {
			limit = { trait = brawny }
			remove_trait = brawny
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = frail }
			health = -1.0
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = frail
		}

		remove_trait = troubled_pregnancy
		set_character_flag = survivor_mom

		spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20549 } }
	}
}

		remove_trait = stressed

		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_priest_comfort
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_shaman_comfort
		clr_character_flag = pregnancy_spouse_comfort
		clr_character_flag = mother_asked_retirement

		if = {
			limit = { multiplayer = yes }
			death = { death_reason = death_troubled_pregnancy }
		}

		spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20551 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20547 # I'll rest just a little more...

		if = {
			limit = { multiplayer = yes }

			tooltip = {
				death = { death_reason = death_troubled_pregnancy }
			}
		}
		else = {
			death = { death_reason = death_troubled_pregnancy }
		}
	}
}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.75 # Young mom is scared
					practical_age < 20
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.75 # Old mom is scared
					practical_age >= 37
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					is_ill = no
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					trait = zealous
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = cynical
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					num_of_children >= 4
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 3
					num_of_children >= 5
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					practical_age >= 35
				}
			}
		}

		# Mother has weird cravings
		random_list = {
			# Yes
			10 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5

					num_of_children < 3

					NOT = {
						any_child = {
							OR = {
								trait = harelip
								trait = ugly
								trait = clubfooted
							}
						}
					}
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5

					has_game_rule = {
						name = pregnancy_flavor
						value = limited
					}
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					trait = hedonist
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = gluttonous
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.35
					trait = temperate
				}

				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20573
					days = 40
					random = 10
				}
			}

			# No
			90 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_children = no
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					num_of_children >= 3
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					num_of_children >= 4
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 3
					num_of_children >= 5
				}
			}
		}

		# Mother receives solace from...
		random_list = {
			# Other sons
			30 = {
				trigger = {
					any_child = {
						age >= 6
						is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					}
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5

					has_game_rule = {
						name = pregnancy_flavor
						value = limited
					}
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.75

					NOT = {
						any_child = {
							age >= 6
							is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
							trait = kind
						}
					}
				}

				random_child = {
					limit = {
						age >= 6
						is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					}

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20574
						months = 4
						random = 20
					}
				}
			}

			# Spouse
			30 = {
				trigger = {
					any_spouse = { is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no }
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.75

					NOT = {
						any_spouse = {
							is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
							trait = kind
						}
					}
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5

					has_game_rule = {
						name = pregnancy_flavor
						value = limited
					}
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.15
					is_ruler = no
					is_main_spouse = no
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					has_character_modifier = adulteress
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
				}

				random_spouse = {
					limit = { is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no }

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20574
						months = 4
						random = 20
					}
				}
			}

			# Lover
			30 = {
				trigger = {
					any_lover = {
						NOT = { is_married = ROOT } # Loving husbands get event above
						is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					}

					is_consort = no
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5

					has_game_rule = {
						name = pregnancy_flavor
						value = limited
					}
				}

				random_lover = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
						is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					}

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20575
						months = 4
						random = 20
					}
				}
			}

			# Spouse organizes Gossiping
			40 = {
				trigger = {
					is_married = yes
					is_main_spouse = yes

					spouse = {
						is_incapable = no
						prisoner = no
					}

					# Only for rulers with vassals (or spouses of rulers)
					OR = {
						is_playable = yes
						spouse = { is_playable = yes }
					}
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5

					has_game_rule = {
						name = pregnancy_flavor
						value = limited
					}
				}

				# Make events less likely to become recurring at every pregnancy
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					num_of_children >= 2
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.35
					num_of_children >= 3
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					num_of_children >= 4
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.15
					num_of_children >= 5
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.65
					trait = gregarious
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					practical_age < 25
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					practical_age >= 35
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					practical_age >= 45
				}

				spouse = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20005 # Fires on husband first
						months = 4
						random = 20
					}
				}
			}

			# Nobody
			40 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 0.85
					has_children = no
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					num_of_children >= 1
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					num_of_children >= 2
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					num_of_children >= 3
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					num_of_children >= 4
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 3
					num_of_children >= 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Mother gets positive omen
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20565
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20565
	picture = GFX_evt_comet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = pregnant
		NOT = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }
	}

	option = { # Interpret
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20565
		tooltip_info = learning

		trigger = { learning >= 10 }

		piety = 300

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = mother_good_omen
			months = 5
		}

		spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20566 } }

		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Chance of a strange positive birth
				limit = { NOT = { has_dynasty_flag = flag_vision_baby } }

				random_list = {
					90 = { } # No vision

					10 = {
						trigger = {
							OR = {
								religion_group = christian
								religion_group = muslim
								religion_openly_tengri_or_reformed_trigger = yes
								religion_openly_norse_or_reformed_trigger = yes
							}
						}

						set_dynasty_flag = flag_vision_baby # Positive

						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20503
							days = 43
							random = 20
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20565

		tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = mother_good_omen
			days = 100
		}

		spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20566 } }

		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Chance of a strange positive birth
				limit = { NOT = { has_dynasty_flag = flag_vision_baby } }

				random_list = {
					99 = { } # No vision

					1 = {
						trigger = {
							OR = {
								religion_group = christian
								religion_group = muslim
								religion_openly_tengri_or_reformed_trigger = yes
								religion_openly_norse_or_reformed_trigger = yes
							}
						}

						set_dynasty_flag = flag_vision_baby	# Positive

						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20503
							days = 43
							random = 20
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
}

# Husband notified
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20568
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20568
	picture = GFX_evt_comet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Reinterpret the signs
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20568
		tooltip_info = learning

		trigger = { learning >= 10 }

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			hidden_effect = { # Remove the older one first
				remove_character_modifier = mother_bad_omen
			}

			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mother_bad_omen
				days = 50
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTBHFP20568_A
			trigger = { is_lover = FROM }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTBHFP20568_B
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_lover = FROM }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_lover = FROM }

			random = {
				chance = 30
				add_trait_stressed_effect = yes
			}
		}

		tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				show_scope_change = no

				add_character_modifier = {
					name = mother_bad_omen
					days = 100
				}

				random = {
					chance = 30

# Mother: Loving husband/child spends time with her
character_event = {

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20578
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_adult = no
				NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20578
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPC20578
		trigger = { is_married = FROM }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = pregnant
		NOT = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }

		FROM = {
			OR = {
				is_married = ROOT
				is_child_of = ROOT
			}

			is_alive = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Chance for mother becoming child's friend
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20578

		trigger = {
			num_of_friends < 3

			NOR = {
				is_married = FROM

				is_rival = FROM
			}
		}

		add_friend = FROM
		remove_trait_silently_stressed_effect = yes

# Mother wanted a boy/girl and she got a...
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20589
	picture = GFX_evt_birth

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20589
		trigger = { has_character_flag = mom_hope_fulfilled }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20589
		trigger = { has_character_flag = mom_hope_unfulfilled }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { is_alive = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_boy }
					FROM = { is_female = no }
				}
				trigger_else = {
					FROM = { is_female = yes }
				}
			}

			set_character_flag = mom_hope_fulfilled
		}
		else = {
			set_character_flag = mom_hope_unfulfilled
		}
	}

	option = { # Success
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20589

		trigger = { has_character_flag = mom_hope_fulfilled }

		tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_kind
			who = FROM
			years = 40
		}
	}

	option = { # Failure - But still likes child
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20589
		tooltip_info = kind

		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = mom_hope_unfulfilled
			trait = kind
		}

		tiered_prestige_negative_effect = yes
	}

	option = { # Failure
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20589

		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = mom_hope_unfulfilled
			NOT = { trait = kind }
		}

		tiered_prestige_negative_effect = yes

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_dislike
			who = FROM
			years = 40
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_boy
		clr_character_flag = mom_hopes_child_girl
		clr_character_flag = mom_hope_fulfilled
		clr_character_flag = mom_hope_unfulfilled
	}
}

# Mother made vow to the Holy Virgin, if child is healthy, time to pay up
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20590
	picture = GFX_evt_virgin_mary_icon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	desc = { # Success - Child is alive and healthy
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20590
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_alive = yes

				NOR = {
					trait = sickly
					trait = inbred
					trait = harelip
					trait = clubfooted
					trait = hunchback
					trait = lisp
					trait = stutter
					trait = ugly
					trait = dwarf
					trait = slow
					trait = imbecile
					trait = weak
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Failure - Child was born but is not healthy
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20590
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_alive = yes

				OR = {
					trait = sickly
					trait = inbred
					trait = harelip
					trait = clubfooted
					trait = hunchback
					trait = lisp
					trait = stutter
					trait = ugly
					trait = dwarf
					trait = slow
					trait = imbecile
					trait = weak
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Critical failure - the child is dead
		text = EVTDESCHFPC20590
		trigger = { FROM = { is_alive = no } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20590

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_alive = yes

				NOR = {
					trait = sickly
					trait = inbred
					trait = harelip
					trait = clubfooted
					trait = hunchback
					trait = lisp
					trait = stutter
					trait = ugly
					trait = dwarf
					trait = slow
					trait = imbecile
					trait = weak
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity }

			remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity

			if = {
				limit = { trait = chaste }
				remove_trait = chaste

				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { trait = celibate } }
					add_trait = celibate
				}

				piety = 200
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { trait = lustful }
				remove_trait = lustful
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = chaste
				piety = 100
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility }

			remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility

			if = {
				limit = { trait = humble }

				add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
				piety = 200
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { trait = proud }
				remove_trait = proud
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = humble
				piety = 100
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity }

			remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity

			if = {
				limit = { trait = charitable }
				wealth = -100
				piety = 300
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { trait = greedy }
				remove_trait = greedy
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = charitable
				piety = 100
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance }

			remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance

			if = {
				limit = { trait = temperate }
				# More later
				piety = 200
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { trait = gluttonous }
				remove_trait = gluttonous
				lose_weight_small_effect = yes
				weight_trait_check_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = temperate
				piety = 100
				lose_weight_small_effect = yes
				weight_trait_check_effect = yes
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25

				has_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity
				trait = lustful
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25

				has_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25

				has_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance
				trait = gluttonous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25

				has_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility
				trait = proud
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # No, I won't keep my vow
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20590

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_alive = yes

				NOR = {
					trait = sickly
					trait = inbred
					trait = harelip
					trait = clubfooted
					trait = hunchback
					trait = lisp
					trait = stutter
					trait = ugly
					trait = dwarf
					trait = slow
					trait = imbecile
					trait = weak
				}
			}
		}

		tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes

		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_modifier

			mother_vow_chastity   = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity }
			mother_vow_temperance = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance }
			mother_vow_charity    = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity }
			mother_vow_humility   = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 15

				# The Virgin strikes son with sickness
				FROM = { character_event = { id = 6063 days = 25 } }
				character_event = { id = HFP.20591 days = 27 } # Notify
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Child is not well or is dead, vow was useless
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20590

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					is_alive = no
					trait = sickly
					trait = inbred
					trait = harelip
					trait = clubfooted
					trait = hunchback
					trait = lisp
					trait = stutter
					trait = ugly
					trait = dwarf
					trait = slow
					trait = imbecile
					trait = weak
				}
			}
		}

		tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes

		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_modifier

			mother_vow_chastity = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_chastity }
			mother_vow_temperance = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_temperance }
			mother_vow_charity = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_charity }
			mother_vow_humility = { remove_character_modifier = mother_vow_humility }
		}
	}
}

# Mother drunk/drugged during pregnancy, child is growing dumb
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20001
	picture = GFX_evt_birth

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20001
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20001
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				trait = slow
				trait = imbecile
			}

			is_alive = yes
			is_incapable = no

			OR = {
				host = { character = ROOT }
				at_location = ROOT
				educator = { character = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Concerned, try stopping the bad habit if still into it
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20001_A # Still drinking
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth }
				trait = drunkard
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20001_B # Still smoking
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth }
				has_character_modifier = hashish_addict
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20001_C # Stopped drinking
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth }
				NOT = { trait = drunkard }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20001_D # Stopped smoking
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth }
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hashish_addict }
			}
		}

		tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes

		tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				show_scope_change = no

				father = {
					show_scope_change = no

					opinion = {
						name = opinion_irresponsible_mother
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = hashish_addict
				FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = withdrawal_symptoms } }

				add_character_modifier = {
					name = withdrawal_symptoms
					months = 5
				}
			}

			random = {
				chance = 20

				add_trait_stressed_effect = yes
				remove_character_modifier = hashish_addict

				if = {
					limit = { has_character_modifier = withdrawal_symptoms }
					remove_character_modifier = withdrawal_symptoms
				}
			}
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				trait = drunkard
				FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth }
			}

			random = {
				chance = 20

				remove_trait = drunkard
				add_trait_stressed_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Not concerned but still addicted
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20001

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth } }
				trait = drunkard
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_character_modifier = hashish_addict
			}

			NOT = { trait = kind }
		}
	}

	after = {
		FROM = {
			clr_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth
			clr_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth
		}
	}
}

# Father: Mother drunk/drugged during pregnancy, child is growing dumb
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20002
	picture = GFX_evt_birth

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20002
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20002
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				trait = slow
				trait = imbecile
			}

			is_alive = yes
			is_incapable = no
			NOT = { trait = bastard }

			OR = {
				host = { character = ROOT }
				at_location = ROOT
				educator = { character = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20002_A # Still drinking
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					has_character_flag = flag_drunk_birth

					mother = {
						trait = drunkard
						is_alive = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20002_B # Still smoking
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					has_character_flag = flag_drugged_birth

					mother = {
						has_character_modifier = hashish_addict
						is_alive = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20002_C # Mother no longer addicted
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					mother = {
						is_alive = yes

						NOR = {
							trait = drunkard
							has_character_modifier = hashish_addict
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20002_D # Mother died in the meantime
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					mother = { is_alive = no }
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			mother = {
				show_scope_change = no

				reverse_opinion = {
					name = opinion_irresponsible_mother
					who = ROOT
					years = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			is_attractive_trigger = no
			is_unattractive_trigger = no
		}
	}

		text = EVTDESCHFPC20003
		trigger = { is_unattractive_trigger = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		}

			limit = { is_main_spouse = yes }

					id = HFP.20004

				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75

		}
