## The Gossiping - Only for rulers or spouses of rulers (COUNT or higher)
# Husband receives event to call other women to entertain wife
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20005
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20005
	picture = GFX_evt_princess_byzantine

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			trait = pregnant
			is_married = ROOT
			is_alive = yes
			is_incapable = no
			is_pilgrim = no
			NOT = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }
		}
	}

	option = { # Call relatives to entertain
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20005

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ROOT = {
					is_ruler = yes

					any_courtier_or_vassal = {
						count >= 2

						is_female = yes
						block_general_event_trigger = no

						OR = {
							is_close_relative = FROM
							is_close_relative = ROOT
						}

						NOR = {
							character = FROM
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}

				FROM = {
					is_ruler = yes

					any_courtier_or_vassal = {
						count >= 2

						is_female = yes
						block_general_event_trigger = no

						OR = {
							is_close_relative = FROM
							is_close_relative = ROOT
						}

						NOR = {
							character = FROM
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = tooltip_HFP20005_A

			FROM = {
				set_character_flag = flag_gossiping_relatives

				character_event = {
					id = HFP.20006 # Notification
					days = 10
					random = 15
				}
			}

			if = { # If husband is ruler, pick from his court
				limit = { is_ruler = yes }

				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						block_general_event_trigger = no

						OR = {
							is_close_relative = FROM
							is_close_relative = ROOT
						}

						NOR = {
							character = FROM
							character = ROOT
						}
					}

					preferred_limit = { ai = no } # Ping player first

					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20010
						days = 5
						random = 5
					}
				}
			}
			else = { # Otherwise, pick from her court

				FROM = {
					random_courtier_or_vassal = {
						limit = {
							is_female = yes
							block_general_event_trigger = no

							OR = {
								is_close_relative = FROM
								is_close_relative = ROOT
							}

							NOR = {
								character = FROM
								character = ROOT
							}
						}

						preferred_limit = { ai = no } # Ping player first

						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20010
							days = 5
							random = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		prestige = 30
		piety = 10

		tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				show_scope_change = no

				add_character_modifier = {
					name = mother_comforted
					months = 2
					stacking = yes
				}

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					name = opinion_swayed_2
					years = 2
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = cruel
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = adulteress }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Hire servants
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20005

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = HFP.20006
				days = 10
				random = 15
				tooltip = tooltip_HFP20005_B
			}

			tooltip = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = mother_comforted
					months = 2
					stacking = yes
				}

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					name = opinion_swayed_2
					years = 2
				}
			}
		}

		scaled_wealth = {
			value = -0.05
			min = -10
			max = -75
		}

		piety = 10

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = cruel
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = adulteress }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Do nothing
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20005

		piety = -10

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = cruel
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = adulteress }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress }
			}
		}
	}
}

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_gossiping_relatives }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	only_capable = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20006
		tooltip_info = gregarious

		trigger = { trait = gregarious }

		remove_trait_silently_depressed_effect = yes

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = mother_comforted
			months = 2
			stacking = yes
		}

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_swayed_2
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20006

		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = gregarious }
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = mother_comforted
			months = 2
			stacking = yes
		}

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_swayed_2
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_character_flag = flag_gossiping_relatives

		hidden_effect = {
			# Fallback events if the mother either has no relative or if the random relative pinged either refused the gossiping or died in the meantime
			random_list = {
				45 = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20007 # Mother enjoys herself, either becomes gregarious or trusting (patient offers chance for +1 learning)
						days = 20
						random = 5
					}
				}

				10 = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20008 # Mother not enjoying herself, either becomes envious or shy (deceitful offers chance for +1 intrigue)
						days = 20
						random = 5
					}
				}

				45 = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20009 # Mother pampered, either becomes content or gluttonous (diligent offers chance for +1 diplomacy)
						days = 20
						random = 5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	only_capable = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }

# Relative: You have been invited to the gossiping
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20010
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20010
	picture = GFX_evt_princess_byzantine

	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_from_from = yes

	trigger = {
		FROMFROM = {
			is_alive = yes
			is_incapable = no
			NOT = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }
		}
	}

	option = { # Very well
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20010

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20011 # Gossip imput
						days = 12
						random = 5
					}
				}

				10 = {
					trigger = {
						num_of_friends < 3
						FROMFROM = { num_of_friends < 3 }

						NOR = {
							is_friend = FROMFROM
							is_rival = FROMFROM
							is_lover = FROMFROM
						}

						opinion = {
							who = FROMFROM
							value >= -30
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = kind
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = charitable
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = gregarious
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = shy
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						FROMFROM = { trait = shy }
					}

					FROMFROM = {
						character_event = {
							id = HFP.20016 # Becoming friends with mother
							days = 12
							random = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
	}

	option = { # No time for it
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20010

		piety = -5

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_offended
			who = FROMFROM
			years = 5
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			trigger = {
				OR = {
					trait = shy
					trait = cruel
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Relative: Notified of mother's reaction
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20015
	picture = GFX_evt_princess_byzantine

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_listening } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_talking } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPC20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_trusting } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPD20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_plotting } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPE20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_envious } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPF20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_shy } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPG20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_learning } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPH20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_content } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPI20015
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_gluttonous } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_A
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_listening } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_B
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_talking } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_C
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_trusting } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_D
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_plotting } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_E
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_envious } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_F
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_shy } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_G
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_learning } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_H
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_content } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20015_I
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_gluttonous } }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_listening } } # Mother took the reward instead

			prestige = 20

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = FROM
				years = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = mother_gossip_talking
						has_character_flag = mother_gossip_trusting
					}
				}
			}

			random = {
				chance = 25
				change_diplomacy = 1
			}

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = FROM
				years = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_plotting } } # Mother took the reward instead

			prestige = 20

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_irritated
				who = FROM
				years = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = mother_gossip_envious
						has_character_flag = mother_gossip_shy
					}
				}
			}

			random = {
				chance = 25
				change_intrigue = 1
			}

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_irritated
				who = FROM
				years = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = mother_gossip_learning } } # Mother took the reward instead

			piety = 10

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = FROM
				years = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = mother_gossip_content
						has_character_flag = mother_gossip_gluttonous
					}
				}
			}

			random = {
				chance = 25
				change_stewardship = 1
			}

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = FROM
				years = 3
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
	}

	after = {
		FROM = {
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_listening
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_talking
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_trusting
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_plotting
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_envious
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_shy
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_learning
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_content
			clr_character_flag = mother_gossip_gluttonous
		}
	}
}

## Post-partum Churching of the Mother (one month after on_birth)
## Only for Catholic Rulers (or main spouses of Rulers) who are married and have produced a(n apparently) legitimate child

# Does mother want to go?
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20018
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20018
	picture = GFX_evt_birth
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	only_capable = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = orthodox
		}

		NOT = { trait = troubled_pregnancy }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = { save_event_target_as = newborn_baby }
	}

	option = { # Yes
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20018

		character_event = {
			id = HFP.20019
			tooltip = tooltip_HFP20018_A
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
	}

	option = { # No
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20018

		remove_trait_zealous_effect = yes
		tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5

			trigger = {
				OR = {
					trait = cynical
					society_member_of = the_satanists
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# What does mother do?
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20019
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20019
	picture = GFX_evt_woman_praying_hf
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Making donation
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20019

		scaled_wealth = {
			value = -0.1
			min = -50
			max = -150
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_churching_wealth

		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
	}

	option = { # Humbling yourself
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20019

		tiered_prestige_negative_effect = yes
		set_character_flag = flag_churching_prestige

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
	}

	option = { # Confessing sins
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20019

		tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes
		set_character_flag = flag_churching_piety

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
	}

	option = { # Nothing
		name = EVTOPTDHFP20019

		tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes
		set_character_flag = flag_churching_nothing

		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				7 = { # Ecstatic vision
					trigger = {
						event_target:newborn_baby = {
							is_alive = yes

							# Jesus knows... somehow
							is_father_real_father = yes
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						trait = cynical
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						has_character_flag = flag_churching_nothing
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						society_member_of = the_satanists
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = trusting
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = zealous
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = celibate
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = chaste
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = temperate
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = humble
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = charitable
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = kind
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = patient
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						trait = diligent
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.15
						piety >= 150
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.15
						piety >= 250
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						piety >= 350
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						piety >= 450
					}

# Response
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20020
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	picture = GFX_evt_woman_praying_hf

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20020
		trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_vision }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20020
		trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_positive }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPC20020
		trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_negative }
	}
	desc = { # As she chokes, mother calls out for real father's name
		text = EVTDESCHFPD20020
		trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_sinner }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = flag_churching_wealth
		clr_character_flag = flag_churching_prestige
		clr_character_flag = flag_churching_piety
		clr_character_flag = flag_churching_nothing
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20020_A
			trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_vision }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20020_B
			trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_positive }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20020_C
			trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_negative }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20020_D
			trigger = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_sinner }
		}

		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_flag

			# Churching resulted in very positive vision:
			flag_churching_vision = {
				tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
				remove_trait_silently_stressed_effect = yes

				random = {
					chance = 30
					remove_trait_cynical_effect = yes
				}

				spouse = {
					character_event = { id = HFP.20021 } # Notify husband
				}

				event_target:newborn_baby = {
					character_event = {
						id = HFP.20027 # Child is blessed
						days = 2500
						random = 250
					}
				}
			}

			# Churching resulted in positive feeling:
			flag_churching_positive = {
				tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes

				spouse = {
					character_event = { id = HFP.20021 } # Notify husband
				}
			}

			# Churching resulted in negative feeling:
			flag_churching_negative = {
				tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes

				random = {
					chance = 40
					add_trait_stressed_effect = yes
				}

				spouse = {
					character_event = { id = HFP.20021 } # Notify husband
				}
			}

			# Churching resulted in very negative omen:
			flag_churching_sinner = {
				tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes

				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { trait = stressed } }
					add_trait = stressed
				}
				else = {
					add_trait_fully_silently_paranoid_effect = yes
				}

				event_target:newborn_baby = {
					prestige = -100

					if = { # If child is not actually illegitimate
						limit = { is_father_real_father = yes }
						set_father = 0
					}
					else = { # If child is actually illegitimate
						real_father_even_if_dead = {
							character_event = { id = HFP.20025 } # Notify real father
						}

						set_father = real_father_even_if_dead
					}
				}

				if = { # If spouse is higher tier, the child is no longer an heir
					limit = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse }

					event_target:newborn_baby = {
						add_trait = bastard
						dynasty = mother_bastard
					}
				}

				spouse = {
					character_event = { id = HFP.20021 } # Notify husband
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		character_event = {
			id = HFP.20026 # Clear all flags
			months = 1
		}
	}
}

# Husband notified of the Churching
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20021
	picture = GFX_evt_woman_praying_hf
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20021
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_vision } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20021
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_positive } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPC20021
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_negative } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPD20021
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_sinner } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_married = ROOT
			is_alive = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Single option because Churching was positive
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20021_A
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_vision } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAHFP20021_B
			trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_positive } }
		}

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = flag_churching_vision
					has_character_flag = flag_churching_positive
				}
			}
		}

		# Churching resulted in very positive vision:
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_vision } }

			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
			remove_trait_silently_stressed_effect = yes
			remove_trait_silently_depressed_effect = yes
		}

		# Churching resulted in positive feeling:
		else = { # flag_churching_positive
			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
			remove_trait_silently_stressed_effect = yes
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = { # Churching was negative, high diplomacy offers comfort
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20021
		tooltip_info = diplomacy

		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_negative }
			diplomacy >= 10
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = { id = HFP.20022 } # Spouse comforted

			tooltip = {
				remove_trait_silently_stressed_effect = yes

				opinion = {
					name = comforted_opinion
					who = ROOT
					years = 2
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { trait = kind }
			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 30
				add_trait_partially_kind_effect = yes
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = { # Churching was negative
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20021

		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_negative }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}

	option = { # Churching was horrible, but husband forgives wife
		name = EVTOPTDHFP20021
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_sinner }

			NOR = {
				trait = cruel
				trait = envious
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			remove_trait_silently_stressed_effect = yes

			opinion = {
				name = comforted_opinion
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20023 } # Spouse forgiven
		}

		tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
		tiered_prestige_negative_effect = yes

		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_trait_fully_kind_effect = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Churching was horrible, and husband is outraged
		name = EVTOPTEHFP20021

		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_churching_sinner }
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = { id = HFP.20024 } # Spouse denounced

			if = {
				limit = { higher_tier_than = ROOT }
				tiered_prestige_negative_effect = yes
			}

			add_character_modifier = {
				name = adulteress
				years = 10
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				trait = paranoid
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = cruel
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
}

# Child is blessed, give random trait
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20027

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			5 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { trait = genius }
				}

				remove_trait = dull
				remove_trait = imbecile
				remove_trait = slow
				remove_trait = quick
				add_trait = genius
			}

			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOR = {
						trait = quick
						trait = genius
					}
				}

				remove_trait = dull
				remove_trait = imbecile
				remove_trait = slow
				add_trait = quick
			}

			15 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { trait = strong }
				}

				remove_trait = weak
				remove_trait = frail
				add_trait = strong
			}

			20 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { trait = attractive }
				}

				remove_trait = ugly
				add_trait = attractive
			}

			25 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { trait = shrewd }
				}

				remove_trait = dull
				remove_trait = imbecile
				remove_trait = slow
				add_trait = shrewd
			}

			25 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { trait = brawny }
				}

				remove_trait = weak
				remove_trait = frail
				add_trait = brawny
			}
		}

		mother = { character_event = { id = HFP.20028 } }
		father = { character_event = { id = HFP.20028 } }
	}
}

								days = 10
								random = 10
							}
						}

						5 = {
							trigger = {
								is_main_spouse = yes
								has_lover = no
								root_attraction_trigger = yes
								attracted_to_root_trigger = yes

								OR = {
									trait = kind
									has_focus = focus_family
									trait = socializer
									trait = gregarious
								}

								ROOT = {
									has_lover = no

									OR = {
										trait = kind
										has_focus = focus_family
										trait = socializer
										trait = gregarious
									}
								}
							}

							character_event = {
								id = HFP.20041 # Falls in love with husband
								days = 10
								random = 10
							}
						}

						25 = { } # Nothing
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = shy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Keep working
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20030

		trigger = { character = FROM }

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Pagan festival of fertility
# Only for Count or higher married rulers (or their main spouse)
# Only for Norse, Finnish, Romuva
# Goddesses mentioned for loc: Freyja (norse), Zemyna (Romuva/baltic), Akka (Finnish)

# Spouse: Organize fertility festival for wife
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20043
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20043
	picture = GFX_evt_viking_throneroom_oldgods
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	only_capable = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_openly_norse_or_reformed_trigger = yes
			religion_openly_baltic_or_reformed_trigger = yes
			religion_openly_finnish_or_reformed_trigger = yes
		}

		FROM = {
			is_married = ROOT
			trait = pregnant
			is_alive = yes
			is_incapable = no
			is_pilgrim = no

			OR = { # Can be of different but similar religion
				religion_openly_norse_or_reformed_trigger = yes
				religion_openly_baltic_or_reformed_trigger = yes
				religion_openly_finnish_or_reformed_trigger = yes
			}

			NOR = {
				trait = troubled_pregnancy
				has_character_modifier = out_traveling
				has_character_modifier = mother_fertility_festival_1
				has_character_modifier = mother_fertility_festival_2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Organize full festival
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20043

		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }

			scaled_wealth = {
				value = -0.25
				min = -25
				max = -100
			}
		}

		tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mother_fertility_festival_2
				years = 4
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_swayed_2
				who = ROOT
				years = 4
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20045 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				wealth < 25
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Give proper offerings
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20043

		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }

			scaled_wealth = {
				value = -0.05
				min = -5
				max = -50
			}
		}

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mother_fertility_festival_1
				years = 2
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_swayed_1
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20044 } # Notify wife, end line
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = greedy
			}

		#	mult_modifier = {
		#		factor = 0.5
		#		wealth < 0
		#	}
		}
	}

	option = { # Not interested
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20043

		tiered_piety_negative_effect = yes

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}
}

# Mother: Festival - Mother of the realm
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20046
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20046
	picture = GFX_evt_homage_hf
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Gregarious
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20046

		if = {
			limit = { trait = gregarious }
			change_diplomacy = 1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = shy }
			remove_trait = shy
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = gregarious
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gregarious

		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
	}

	option = { # Kind
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20046

		if = {
			limit = { trait = kind }
			change_diplomacy = 1
		}
		else = {
			add_trait_partially_silently_kind_effect = yes
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_kind

		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
	}

	option = { # Piety
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20046

		tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_piety

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }
			spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20054 } } # Spouse notified
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gregarious
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_kind
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_piety
		}
	}
}

# Mother: Festival - A goddess am I
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20047
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20047
	picture = GFX_evt_homage_hf
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Proud
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20047

		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = proud }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { trait = humble }
			remove_trait = humble
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = proud
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_proud

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}

	option = { # Ambitious
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20047

		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = ambitious }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { trait = content }
			remove_trait = content
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = ambitious
		}

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = lunatic } }

			random = {
				chance = 30

				add_trait = lunatic
				character_event = { id = HFP.20048 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_ambitious

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}

	option = { # Piety
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20047

		tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes
		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_prestige

		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }
			spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20054 } } # Spouse notified
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_proud
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_ambitious
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_prestige
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

			gain_weight_small_effect = yes
			weight_trait_check_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_trait_partially_silently_gluttonous_effect = yes
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gluttonous

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}

	option = { # Drunkard
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20052

		if = {
			limit = { trait = drunkard }

			gain_weight_small_effect = yes
			weight_trait_check_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = drunkard
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_drunkard

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
	}

	after = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = mother_festival_blessing
			years = 5
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }
			spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20054 } } # Spouse notified
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gluttonous
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_drunkard
		}
	}
}

# Mother: Festival - Godly virtues
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20053
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20053
	picture = GFX_evt_homage_hf
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Chaste
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20053

		if = {
			limit = { trait = lustful }
			remove_trait = lustful
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = chaste }
			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = chaste
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_chaste

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Lustful
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20053

		if = {
			limit = { trait = chaste }
			remove_trait = chaste
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = lustful }
			tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = lustful
		}

		set_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_lustful

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				trait = chaste
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }
			spouse = { character_event = { id = HFP.20054 } } # Spouse notified
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_chaste
			clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_lustful
		}
	}
}

	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPN20054
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_lustful } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20054_A

		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gregarious } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gregarious }
			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_kind } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_kind }
			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_piety } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_piety }
			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_proud } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_proud }
			tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_ambitious } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_ambitious }
			tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_prestige } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_prestige }
			tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_peasants } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_peasants }

			if = {
				limit = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON }

				capital_scope = {
					show_scope_change = no

					add_province_modifier = {
						name = fertility_festival_province
						years = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_vassals } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_vassals }

			if = {
				limit = { higher_real_tier_than = BARON }

				custom_tooltip = {
					text = tooltip_HFPA20054

					any_courtier_or_vassal = {
						limit = {
							religion = ROOT
							is_adult = yes

							OR = {
								is_theocracy = yes
								trait = zealous
								trait = theologian
							}
						}

						character_event = { id = HFP.20051 }

						opinion = {
							name = opinion_mother_goddess
							who = FROM
							years = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gluttonous } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_gluttonous }
			tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_drunkard } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_drunkard }
			tiered_prestige_reward_effect = yes

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_chaste } }

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_chaste }
			tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes

		}
		else_if = {

			FROM = { clr_character_flag = flag_mother_festival_lustful }

		}
	}
}

# Hollow child gains specific trait
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20057
	desc = EVTDESCHFPA20057
	picture = GFX_evt_child_reading

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_yearly_childhood_pulse
	hide_from = yes

	has_character_flag = flag_hollow_child_primed
	min_age = 7
	max_age = 10

	trigger = {
		trait = malnourished

		NOR = {
			has_nickname = nick_the_pale_prince
			has_nickname = nick_the_hollow
			has_character_flag = flag_hollow_child
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20057

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = brooding
					trait = envious
				}
			}
			change_intrigue = 2
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Conclave" }
				add_trait = brooding
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = envious
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20057

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = timid
					trait = shy
				}
			}
			change_intrigue = 2
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Conclave" }
				add_trait = timid
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = shy
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
	}

	after = {
		clr_character_flag = flag_hollow_child_primed
		set_character_flag = flag_hollow_child

		if = {
			limit = { has_minor_title = title_prince }
			give_nickname = nick_the_pale_prince
		}
		else = {
			give_nickname = nick_the_hollow
		}
	}
}

			add_trait = brave
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hollow_child_brave
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	option = {

			limit = { trait = erudite }
			change_learning = 2
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = erudite
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hollow_child_erudite
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20058

		if = {
			limit = { trait = cruel }
			change_intrigue = 2
		}
		else = {
			remove_trait_silently_kind_effect = yes
			add_trait = cruel
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = hollow_child_cruel
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	after = {
		character_event = {
			id = HFP.20059
			days = 5
		}

		clr_character_flag = flag_hollow_child
	}
}

# Spouse: Mother aborted child to avoid hard pregnancy
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20061
	picture = GFX_evt_quarrel

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPA20061
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = adulteress
					has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCHFPB20061
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOR = {
					has_character_modifier = adulteress
					has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Not my problem
		name = EVTOPTAHFP20061

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = adulteress
					has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = { # Denounce her
		name = EVTOPTBHFP20061

		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = kind }

			FROM = {
				NOR = {
					has_character_modifier = adulteress
					has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
				}
			}
		}

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_executed_child
			who = ROOT
			years = 10
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			tooltip = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = cowardly_infanticide
					years = 100
				}

				tiered_prestige_negative_effect = yes
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20062 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				religion_group = christian
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Forgive her
		name = EVTOPTCHFP20061

		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = cruel }

			FROM = {
				NOR = {
					has_character_modifier = adulteress
					has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_forgiven
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}

			character_event = { id = HFP.20063 }
		}

		tiered_piety_reward_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Do not care
		name = EVTOPTDHFP20061

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOR = {
					has_character_modifier = adulteress
					has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Cleanup on_birth event to remove illegitimate trait gained when a wife gives birth after the death of her husband
character_event = {
	id = HFP.20068

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_birth
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		father_even_if_dead = {
			is_alive = no
			NOT = { trait = eunuch }
		}

		mother_even_if_dead = {
			NOR = {
				has_character_modifier = adulteress
				has_character_modifier = incestuous_adulteress
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_trait = bastard
		remove_trait = legit_bastard
	}
}
